Fresh seafood with good cooking technique,,,, this place always does good job. This time, Lobster head chao was my choice of the night, so yummy!!
===***===
When I receive somebody from Japan, this place is one of my choice. They always serve with fresh and good food and atmosphere. One of their signature menue, fish rice paper roll, was good as always and prawn cooked with coconut juice, just about right sweetness with cooked texture. Don't forget to order scallop grilled with white sauce, their Sauce Bechamel is very very tasty!! This time, I learned to sprinkle rice cracker on hotpot and it was tasty experince!! Well, there were 2 negative points this time,,,, Squid grilled with salt and chili, too hot this time and crab stir fried with vermicelli was not quite good as always,,, crab flavor was not strong enough,,,. Overall, I still well recommend this place. (I hope their recent financial situation won't affect to their food they serve..)

===***===
Came here for dinner with some friends. We were told that this place tasted like italian food from italy rather than north american italian food and boy did it live up to our expectations. The appetizers of antipasto was amazing. The fresh bread, olive oil and balsalmic vinegrette was just how i remembered eating it in Florence. My husband had the wagu beef steak and they cooked it perfectly the way he likes it (chicago blue rare) and i had the lamb popsicles for dinner (again cooked perfectly to medium well). We shared the spaghetti with clams and it was so yummy! 

We had chocolate cake and tiramisu for dessert which again was good. 

Overall, food was amazing, beautiful restaurant, friendly staff but you are paying north american prices for food. Would recommend coming here for special occasions or if youre in the mood to splurge on dinner.

I am totally disappointed with the food quality standard of the buffet here compared to other hotels around district 1. Crab, blue swimming crab totally not fresh. Pork sausage is so salty that I stop on the first bite. Vegetable minestrone soup is very salty as well. Sweet and sour fish -- can't taste the sweetness nor the sourness. Only plus is the lobster and prawns which is slightly fresher than other seafood. Even simple fruits like guava are inedible. I don't know what happen to the buffet here. It used to be one of the best 15 years ago but now they are nowhere even near to local restaurant buffet standard.
